        <div class="mw-references-wrap">
         <ol class="references"> 
          <li id="cite_note-all-18"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-all_18-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-all_18-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-all_18-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-all_18-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Includes IP users. Any permission granted to all users will be inherited by the other user groups.</span> </li> 
          <li id="cite_note-reg-19"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-reg_19-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-reg_19-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-reg_19-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-reg_19-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Any permission granted to registered accounts will be inherited by the other (registered) user groups.</span> </li> 
          <li id="cite_note-other-20"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-other_20-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-other_20-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-other_20-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-other_20-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Any user listed in this column has the relevant permission. Italics indicate a global permission.</span> </li> 
          <li id="cite_note-AC-21"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-AC_21-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-AC_21-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Only autoconfirmed</span> </li> 
          <li id="cite_note-GRP-22"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-GRP_22-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-GRP_22-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-GRP_22-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-GRP_22-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Per <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Global_rights_policy" title="Wikipedia:Global rights policy">Wikipedia:Global rights policy</a>, Global rollbackers are only allowed to use this right in the context of counter-vandalism efforts</span> </li> 
         </ol>
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>The userright <i>proxyunbannable</i> is assigned to administrators but has no effect since WMF wikis use <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Extension:TorBlock" class="extiw" title="mw:Extension:TorBlock">mw:Extension:TorBlock</a> instead of the default MediaWiki proxy blocker. Administrators are not exempt from tor blocks, only users in the IP block exemptions usergroup are, due to the <i>torunblocked</i> userright.</li> 
       <li>IPs and new users are limited to 8 edits per minute. Autoconfirmed or confirmed users who are in no usergroup with the <i>noratelimit</i> userright are limited to 8 moves per minute. Rollbackers in the same situation are limited to 100 rollbacks per minute.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[18]</a></sup> Account creations are subject to an IP based limit, <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:$wgAccountCreationThrottle" class="extiw" title="mw:Manual:$wgAccountCreationThrottle">set at 6</a> for WMF wikis, but users with <i>noratelimit</i> are unaffected.</li>
      </ul>

       <p><small><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_1"><b><a href="#ref_1">^1</a></b></span> Because bureaucrats were <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_comment/Granting_bureaucrats_the_technical_ability_to_remove_the_admin_flag" title="Wikipedia:Requests for comment/Granting bureaucrats the technical ability to remove the admin flag">granted</a> the ability to do this, stewards would refer most ordinary requests for removal of the sysop permission to them, but retain the right to remove the sysop permission when appropriate (such as emergencies or requests from the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Arbitration_Committee" title="Wikipedia:Arbitration Committee">Arbitration Committee</a>).</small> <br> </p> 
      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Former_levels">Former levels</span></h2> 
      <p><span class="anchor" id="Course_coordinator,_instructor,_online_and_campus_volunteer"></span><span class="anchor" id="Afttest_and_Afttest-hide"></span><span class="anchor" id="ep-staff"></span><span class="anchor" id="ep-admin"></span><span class="anchor" id="ep-campus-ambassador"></span><span class="anchor" id="ep-online-ambassador"></span><span class="anchor" id="ep-instructor"></span> </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><i>Course coordinator, instructor, online and campus volunteer</i> 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          Enabled users to manage course pages in the "Education Program:" namespace, which was <a class="external text" href="https://outreach.wikimedia.org/wiki/Education/News/January_2018/Education_Extension_scheduled_shutdown">shutdown in June 2018</a>
         </dd>
        </dl></li> 
       <li><i>Afttest and Afttest-hide</i> 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          Only granted by WMF staff, these enabled users to delete and/or hide <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AFT5" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:AFT5">article feedback</a>. Removed in March 2014 after a one-year run.
         </dd>
        </dl></li> 
       <li><i>EP staff, administrator, campus-ambassador, online-ambassador, and instructor</i> 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          Used by users to coordinate and work with students, instructors, and institutions as part of the <a class="external text" href="https://outreach.wikimedia.org/wiki/Education/About">education program</a>. Deprecated since 2013.
         </dd>
        </dl></li>
      </ul>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span></h2> 
      <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1011085734">
      <div class="reflist"> 
       <div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns">
        <ol class="references"> 
         <li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">See wgTorAutoConfirmAge and wgTorAutoConfirmCount in <a class="external free" href="https://noc.wikimedia.org/conf/CommonSettings.php.txt">https://noc.wikimedia.org/conf/CommonSettings.php.txt</a></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-2">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In accordance with <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_comment/Event_coordinator_proposal" title="Wikipedia:Requests for comment/Event coordinator proposal">this RfC</a>, event coordinators may only grant the 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">confirmed</span> flag to editors who actually participate in an outreach event.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-3">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Their most recent edit must have been made after 5&nbsp;April&nbsp;2016, when <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;offset=20160405231900&amp;type=rights&amp;user=&amp;page=&amp;tagfilter=&amp;subtype=autopromote">
            <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">extendedconfirmed</span> was implemented</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Special:PermanentLink/782473728#Clarification_request:_Arbitration_motions_regarding_extended_confirmed_protection_(May_2017)" title="Special:PermanentLink/782473728">28 May 2017 clarification request</a></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-5">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/MediaWiki" title="MediaWiki">MediaWiki</a> <a class="external text" href="https://phabricator.wikimedia.org/diffusion/MW/browse/master/includes/DefaultSettings.php">default settings</a> are that the 'bureaucrats' group has the 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">userrights</span> flag (giving access to <a href="/wiki/Special:UserRights" title="Special:UserRights">Special:UserRights</a>) and can add or remove any flags. However this can be modified by <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:$wgAddGroups" class="extiw" title="mw:Manual:$wgAddGroups">mw:Manual:$wgAddGroups</a> and <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:$wgRemoveGroups" class="extiw" title="mw:Manual:$wgRemoveGroups">mw:Manual:$wgRemoveGroups</a> to restrict adding/removing flags to specified ones. Wikimedia's settings file <a class="external text" href="https://noc.wikimedia.org/conf/highlight.php?file=InitialiseSettings.php">uses these</a>, and by default bureaucrats can only <i>remove</i> 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">bot</span> flags and <i>add</i> 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">administrator, bureaucrat</span> and 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">bot</span> flags. English Wikipedia, or 'enwiki', settings additionally permit adding 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">accountcreator</span> and removal of 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">ipblock-exempt</span> and 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">accountcreator</span>; which administrators can do anyway, and removal of 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">sysop</span>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Since August 2011, per <a href="https://phabricator.wikimedia.org/T20390" class="extiw" title="phabricator:T20390">T20390</a></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r999302996">.mw-parser-output cite.citation{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .citation q{quotes:"\"""\"""'""'"}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-free a,.mw-parser-output .citation .cs1-lock-free a{background:linear-gradient(transparent,transparent),url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/65/Lock-green.svg")right 0.1em center/9px no-repeat}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-limited a,.mw-parser-output .id-lock-registration a,.mw-parser-output .citation .cs1-lock-limited a,.mw-parser-output .citation .cs1-lock-registration a{background:linear-gradient(transparent,transparent),url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d6/Lock-gray-alt-2.svg")right 0.1em center/9px no-repeat}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-subscription a,.mw-parser-output .citation .cs1-lock-subscription a{background:linear-gradient(transparent,transparent),url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/aa/Lock-red-alt-2.svg")right 0.1em center/9px no-repeat}.mw-parser-output .cs1-subscription,.mw-parser-output .cs1-registration{color:#555}.mw-parser-output .cs1-subscription span,.mw-parser-output .cs1-registration span{border-bottom:1px dotted;cursor:help}.mw-parser-output .cs1-ws-icon a{background:linear-gradient(transparent,transparent),url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/4/4c/Wikisource-logo.svg")right 0.1em center/12px no-repeat}.mw-parser-output code.cs1-code{color:inherit;background:inherit;border:none;padding:inherit}.mw-parser-output .cs1-hidden-error{display:none;font-size:100%}.mw-parser-output .cs1-visible-error{font-size:100%}.mw-parser-output .cs1-maint{display:none;color:#33aa33;margin-left:0.3em}.mw-parser-output .cs1-format{font-size:95%}.mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-left,.mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-wl-left{padding-left:0.2em}.mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-right,.mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-wl-right{padding-right:0.2em}.mw-parser-output .citation .mw-selflink{font-weight:inherit}</style><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Project:Account_creators">"Project:Account creators"</a>. <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Project:About" class="extiw" title="mediawikiwiki:Project:About">MediaWikiWiki</a>. 2015<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">2015-02-01</span></span>. <q><a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:DefaultSettings.php" class="extiw" title="mw:Manual:DefaultSettings.php">DefaultSettings.php</a> grants the <code>noratelimit</code> <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:User_rights" class="extiw" title="mw:Manual:User rights">user right</a> to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Bureaucrats" title="Wikipedia:Bureaucrats">bureaucrats</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Administrators" title="Wikipedia:Administrators">sysops</a>.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Project%3AAccount+creators&amp;rft.pub=MediaWikiWiki&amp;rft.date=2015&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.mediawiki.org%2Fwiki%2FProject%3AAccount_creators&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AWikipedia%3AUser+access+levels" class="Z3988"></span></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-8"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-8">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This flag only grants the exempted user to <i>edit</i> behind the IP address. IP block exempt users are not able to create accounts while behind an IP address that is also blocked with the "Prevent account creation" option enabled.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Administrators and bots are not affected by <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTOBLOCK" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:AUTOBLOCK">autoblocks</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:HARDBLOCK" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:HARDBLOCK">hard IP address blocks</a>. However, the ipblock-exempt flag <i>must</i> be added to the administrator or bot account as a separate user right to allow them to edit from IP addresses affected by <a href="/wiki/Tor_(anonymity_network)#Tor_exit_node_block" class="mw-redirect" title="Tor (anonymity network)">Tor blocks</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-10"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-10">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">See this RfC at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:Interface_administrators/Archive_3#Allow_non-admins_to_request_access?" title="Wikipedia talk:Interface administrators/Archive 3">Wikipedia talk:Interface administrators/Archive 3#Allow non-admins to request access?</a></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-11">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:PermanentLink/18694289" class="extiw" title="meta:Special:PermanentLink/18694289">WMF 2FA requirement as published on Meta-Wiki</a></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-wmf-12"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-wmf_12-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-wmf_12-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">The Wikimedia Foundation has <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/545773892" title="Special:Diff/545773892">stated</a> that an "RfA or RfA-identical process" is required for users to be granted access to deleted revisions.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Although there are two <a href="/wiki/Founder_of_Wikipedia" title="Founder of Wikipedia">co-founders</a>, <a href="/wiki/User:Jimbo_Wales" title="User:Jimbo Wales">User:Jimbo Wales</a> is the only member of this group—see <a href="/wiki/Special:ListUsers/founder" title="Special:ListUsers/founder">Special:ListUsers/founder</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-14"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-14">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="https://phabricator.wikimedia.org/T253420" class="extiw" title="phab:T253420">Phabricator Task T253420: Add 'deletedtext' right to user group 'researchers'</a></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-15"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-15">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The group has access to the 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">browsearchive</span>, 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">deletedhistory</span> and 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">deletedtext</span> rights, as well 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886049734"><span class="monospaced">apihighlimits</span> (<a href="/wiki/Special:ListGroupRights#researcher" title="Special:ListGroupRights">Special:ListGroupRights#researcher</a>)</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-16"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-16">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">See the RfC at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:User_access_levels/Archive_2#Rights_of_indef_blocked_users" title="Wikipedia talk:User access levels/Archive 2">Wikipedia talk:User access levels/Archive 2#Rights of indef blocked users</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-17"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-17">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">See the RfC at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_comment/User_rights_of_(site)_banned_users" title="Wikipedia:Requests for comment/User rights of (site) banned users">Wikipedia:Requests for comment/User rights of (site) banned users</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-23"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-23">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The API query <a class="external free" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/api.php?action=query&amp;meta=userinfo&amp;uiprop=ratelimits%7Cgroups">https://en.wikipedia.org/w/api.php?action=query&amp;meta=userinfo&amp;uiprop=ratelimits%7Cgroups</a> can be used to check those values.</span> </li> 
        </ol>
       </div>
